<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200"></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/car" class="extiw" title="w:car">car</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/car" class="extiw" title="w:car">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/British_English" class="extiw" title="w:British English">UK</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/kɑː/</span></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Etymology 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/carre#Middle_English" title="carre">carre</a></i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/carre#Old_French" title="carre">carre</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norman" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norman">Old Northern French</a></span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/char#Old_French" title="char">char</a></i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/carra#Latin" title="carra">carra</a></i>, neuter plural of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/carrus#Latin" title="carrus">carrus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">four-wheeled baggage wagon</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gaulish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gaulish language">Gaulish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cel-gau"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Gaulish/karros" title="Reconstruction:Gaulish/karros">*karros</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Celtic/karros" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Celtic/karros">*karros</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wagon</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/carr#English" title="carr">carr</a></span> (<i>archaic</i>)</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">car</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/cars#English" title="cars">cars</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A wheeled vehicle that moves independently, with at least three wheels, powered mechanically, steered by a driver and mostly for personal <a href="/wiki/transportation" title="transportation">transportation</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/auto#English" title="auto">auto</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/motorcar#English" title="motorcar">motorcar</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/vehicle#English" title="vehicle">vehicle</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/automobile#English" title="automobile">automobile</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">US</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/motor#English" title="motor">motor</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Britain, colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/carriage#English" title="carriage">carriage</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; <i>see also</i> <a href="/wiki/Thesaurus:automobile" title="Thesaurus:automobile">Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">automobile</span></a></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">She drove her <b>car</b> to the mall.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2005</b>,  Jordan Houston, Darnell Carlton, Paul Beauregard, Premro Smith, Marlon Goodwin, David Brown, and Willie Hutchinson (lyrics),  “Stay Fly”, in  <cite>Most Known Unknown</cite>‎<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://genius.com/Three-6-mafia-stay-fly-lyrics">[1]</a></sup>, Sony BMG, performed by Three 6 Mafia (featuring Young Buck, 8 Ball, and MJG):</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I'm a stunt; ride in the <b>car</b> with some bump in the trunk.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2006</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edwin_Black" class="extiw" title="w:Edwin Black">Edwin Black</a>,  chapter 1, in  <cite>Internal Combustion</cite>‎<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL4103950W">[2]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">If successful, Edison and Ford—in 1914—would move society away from the ever more expensive and then universally known killing hazards of gasoline <b>cars</b>:&nbsp;[…] .</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#dated" title="Appendix:Glossary">dated</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/wheeled" title="wheeled">wheeled</a> <a href="/wiki/vehicle" title="vehicle">vehicle</a>, drawn by a <a href="/wiki/horse" title="horse">horse</a> or other animal; a <a href="/wiki/chariot" title="chariot">chariot</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><b>1594</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Christopher_Marlowe" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Christopher Marlowe">Christopher Marlowe</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_II_(play)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Edward II (play)">Edward II</a></i>, London: William Jones,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://name.umdl.umich.edu/A07018.0001.001">[3]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>It shall suffice me to enioy your loue,</dd>
<dd>Which whiles I haue, I thinke my selfe as great,</dd>
<dd>As <i>Caesar</i> riding in the Romaine streete,</dd>
<dd>With captiue kings at his triumphant <b>Carre</b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li>c. <b>1606</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Antony_and_Cleopatra" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Antony and Cleopatra">Antony and Cleopatra</a></i>, Act IV, Scene 8,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.opensourceshakespeare.org/views/plays/play_view.php?WorkID=antonycleo&amp;Scope=entire&amp;pleasewait=1&amp;msg=pl">[4]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>He has deserved it [armour], were it carbuncled</dd>
<dd>Like holy Phoebus’ <b>car</b>.</dd></dl></li></ul>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brummie" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Brummie">Birmingham</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#obsolete" title="Appendix:Glossary">obsolete</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A four-wheeled <a href="/wiki/cab" title="cab">cab</a>, as opposed to a (two-wheeled) <a href="/wiki/Hansom_cab" title="Hansom cab">Hansom cab</a>.</li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/rail_transport" title="rail transport">rail transport</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly <a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a>, <a href="/wiki/American_English" title="American English">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An unpowered unit in a <a href="/wiki/railroad" title="railroad">railroad</a> train.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/railcar#English" title="railcar">railcar</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/wagon#English" title="wagon">wagon</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The conductor coupled the <b>cars</b> to the locomotive.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/rail_transport" title="rail transport">rail transport</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> an individual vehicle, powered or unpowered, in a <a href="/wiki/multiple_unit" title="multiple unit">multiple unit</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The 11:10 to London was operated by a 4-<b>car</b> diesel multiple unit.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li class="mw-empty-elt"></li><li class="senseid" id="English-passenger-carrying_unit_in_a_subway_or_elevated_train,_whether_powered_or_not"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/rail_transport" title="rail transport">rail transport</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A passenger-carrying unit in a <a href="/wiki/subway" title="subway">subway</a> or elevated train, whether powered or not.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">From the frontmost <b>car</b> of the subway, he filmed the progress through the tunnel.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/rough" title="rough">rough</a> <a href="/wiki/unit" title="unit">unit</a> of quantity approximating the amount which would fill a <a href="/wiki/railroad" title="railroad">railroad</a> car.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/carload#English" title="carload">carload</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/wagonload#English" title="wagonload">wagonload</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">We ordered five hundred <b>cars</b> of gypsum.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>The moving, load-carrying component of an <a href="/wiki/elevator" title="elevator">elevator</a> or other <a href="/wiki/cable" title="cable">cable</a>-drawn transport mechanism.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Fix the <b>car</b> of the express elevator - the door is sticking.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>The passenger-carrying portion of certain <a href="/wiki/amusement_park" title="amusement park">amusement park</a> rides, such as <a href="/wiki/Ferris_wheel" title="Ferris wheel">Ferris wheels</a>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/carriage#English" title="carriage">carriage</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The most exciting part of riding a Ferris wheel is when your <b>car</b> goes over the top.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>The part of an <a href="/wiki/airship" title="airship">airship</a>, such as a <a href="/wiki/balloon" title="balloon">balloon</a> or <a href="/wiki/dirigible" title="dirigible">dirigible</a>, which houses the passengers and control apparatus.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/gondola#English" title="gondola">gondola</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/basket#English" title="basket">basket</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">balloons only</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl>
<ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1850</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Wise_(balloonist)" class="extiw" title="w:John Wise (balloonist)">John Wise</a>,  <cite><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=sfYOAAAAYAAJ">A System of Aeronautics</a></cite>, page 152:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Everything being apparently in readiness now, I stepped into the <b>car</b> of the balloon, <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1912</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arthur_Conan_Doyle" class="extiw" title="w:Arthur Conan Doyle">Sir Arthur Conan Doyle</a>,  <cite>The Lost World</cite>‎<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.gutenberg.org/cache/epub/139/pg139.txt">[5]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"What about a<b> car?</b>" "The<b> car </b>will be my next care. I have already planned how it is to be made and attached. Meanwhile I will simply show you how capable my apparatus is of supporting the weight of each of us."</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/sailing#Noun" title="sailing">sailing</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A sliding fitting that runs along a track.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1995</b>,  Ken Textor,  <cite>The New Book of Sail Trim</cite>‎<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=2JIbS0c1XPwC">[6]</a></sup>, <small><a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0924486813" title="Special:BookSources/0924486813">→ISBN</a></small>, page 201:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">On boats 25 feet or more, it is best to mount a mast <b>car</b> and track on the front of the mast so you can adjust the height of the pole above the deck</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The aggregate of desirable characteristics of a car.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Buy now! You can get more <b>car</b> for your money.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A floating perforated box for living fish.</li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Etymology 2">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Etymology unclear, but probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/karzijan%C4%85&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/karzijaną (page does not exist)">*karzijaną</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to turn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/gers-&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/gers- (page does not exist)">*gers-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bend, turn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/cair#English" title="cair">cair</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to turn, go</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/char#English" title="char">char</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to turn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/keren#Dutch" title="keren">keren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to turn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/Kehre#German" title="Kehre">Kehre</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">turn, bend</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Shakespeare">Shakespeare</a> had something of a fondness for verbalizing nouns, and sometimes even substantivizing verbs. However, anything other than a "turn" does not seem to make any sense within the broader context of the cited Sonnet.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">car</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/cars#English" title="cars">cars</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#obsolete" title="Appendix:Glossary">obsolete</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/turn" title="turn">turn</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><b>1609</b> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, Sonnet 7,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.opensourceshakespeare.org/views/sonnets/sonnet_view.php?Sonnet=7">[7]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>But when from highmost pitch, with weary <b>car</b>,</dd>
<dd>Like feeble age, he reeleth from the day, <small>(after the sun reaches the zenith it, with a <i>weary</i> turn, begins to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/reel#English" title="reel">reel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to roll</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (downwards))</small></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Etymology 3">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Cons-cells.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Cons-cells.svg/220px-Cons-cells.svg.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="54" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Cons-cells.svg/330px-Cons-cells.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Cons-cells.svg/440px-Cons-cells.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="685" data-file-height="167"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Cons-cells.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Diagram for the list (42 69 613). The <a class="mw-selflink selflink">car</a> of the first <a href="/wiki/cons" title="cons">cons</a> is 42, and the <a href="/wiki/cdr" title="cdr">cdr</a> points the next cons.</div></div></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#acronym" title="Appendix:Glossary">Acronym</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/content#English" title="content"><b>c</b>ontents</a> of the <a href="/wiki/address#English" title="address"><b>a</b>ddress</a> part of <a href="/wiki/register#English" title="register"><b>r</b>egister</a>  number</i>. Note that it was based on original hardware and has no meaning today.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">car</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/cars#English" title="cars">cars</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/programming#Noun" title="programming">programming</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The first part of a <a href="/wiki/cons" title="cons">cons</a> in <a href="/wiki/LISP" title="LISP">LISP</a>. The first element of a list.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><dl><dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/cdr#English" title="cdr">cdr</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms holonym"><span class="defdate">Holonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/cons#English" title="cons">cons</a></span></span></dd></dl>
<ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2000</b>,  Matt Kaufmann; Panagiotis Manolios; J Strother Moore,  <cite>Computer-aided reasoning: an approach</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The elements of a list are the successive <b>cars</b> along the "cdr chain." That is, the elements are the <b>car</b>, the <b>car</b> of the cdr, the <b>car</b> of the cdr of the cdr, etc.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Aromanian">Aromanian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Aromanian">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms_2">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="rup"><a href="/wiki/caru#Aromanian" title="caru">caru</a></span></li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/carrus#Latin" title="carrus">carrus</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gaulish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gaulish language">Gaulish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cel-gau"><a href="/w/index.php?title=karros&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="karros (page does not exist)">karros</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Romanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Romanian language">Romanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ro"><a href="/wiki/car#Romanian" title="car">car</a></i>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Czech">Czech</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Czech">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href="/wiki/%D1%86%D1%A3%D1%81%D0%B0%D1%80%D1%8C#Old_Church_Slavonic" title="цѣсарь">цѣсарь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">cěsarĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,  from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic language">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Slavic/c%C4%9Bsa%C5%99%D1%8C" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Slavic/cěsařь">*cěsařь</a></i>, from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Germanic languages">Germanic</a></span> language, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kaisaraz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kaisaraz">*kaisaraz</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/Caesar#Latin" title="Caesar">Caesar</a></i>.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Etymology 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/quer#Old_French" title="quer">quer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">as, since, because, for</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/quare#Latin" title="quare">quārē</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">how; why</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Catalan_language" class="extiw" title="w:Catalan language">Catalan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ca"><a href="/wiki/car#Catalan" title="car">car</a></i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction_2">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Conjunction">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fr">car</strong>
</p>
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/as" title="as">as</a>, <a href="/wiki/since" title="since">since</a>, <a href="/wiki/because" title="because">because</a>, <a href="/wiki/for" title="for">for</a>
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#c." title="Appendix:Glossary"><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></a></i> <b>1656–1662</b>,  Blaise Pascal,  “<i>Dossier de travail</i> - Fragment n° 10 / 35”, in  <cite>Pensées</cite> [<cite>Thoughts</cite>]‎<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.penseesdepascal.fr/I/I10-moderne.php">[8]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="fr"><b>Car</b> dans la création de l’homme Adam en était le témoin et le dépositaire de la promesse du sauveur qui devait naître de la femme, lorsque les hommes étaient encore si proches de la Création qu’ils ne pouvaient avoir oublié leur création et leur chute.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>For</b> in the creation of man, Adam was the witness and the depositary of the promise of the saviour who would be born of woman, when the men were still so close to the Creation that they could not have forgotten their creation and their fall.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr">J’ai ouvert mon parapluie <b>car</b> il pleuvait.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I opened my umbrella <b>because</b> it was raining.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Synonyms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/parce_que#French" title="parce que">parce que</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in some contexts</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span id="attentionseekingfr" class="attentionseeking" lang="fr" title="Someone left a comment saying &quot;This is not a perfect synonym, a usage note by a native speaker would be good&quot;"></span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Etymology 2">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/car#English" title="car">car</a></i>, itself borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span> and the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norman" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norman">Old Northern French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/car#Old_French" title="car">car</a></i>, variant of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/char#Old_French" title="char">char</a></i>. <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#doublet" title="Appendix:Glossary">Doublet</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/char#French" title="char">char</a></i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fr">car</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-fr p-form-of" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/cars#French" title="cars">cars</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a single-decked long-distance, or privately hired, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/bus#English" title="bus">bus</a></span>, a <a href="/wiki/coach" title="coach">coach</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr">Les élèves vont à l’école en <b>car</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The pupils go to school by <b>coach</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Irish">Irish</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Irish">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Irish">Old Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sga"><a href="/wiki/caraid#Old_Irish" title="caraid">caraid</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Celtic/kareti" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Celtic/kareti">*kareti</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to love</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/keh%E2%82%82-" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/keh₂-">*keh₂-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to desire, wish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_5">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Irish_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Irish pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/karˠ/</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Verb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_6">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Polish">Polish</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=65" title="Edit section: Polish">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200"></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">Polish <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="pl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/pl:car" class="extiw" title="w:pl:car">car</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/pl:car" class="extiw" title="w:pl:car">Wikipedia <sup>pl</sup></a></span></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_7">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=66" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href="/wiki/%D1%86%D0%B0%D1%80%D1%8C#Russian" title="царь">царь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">carʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic language">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Slavic/c%C4%9Bsa%C5%99%D1%8C" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Slavic/cěsařь">*cěsařь</a></i>, from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Germanic languages">Germanic</a></span> language, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kaisaraz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kaisaraz">*kaisaraz</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/Caesar#Latin" title="Caesar">Caesar</a></i>. <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#doublet" title="Appendix:Glossary">Doublet</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl"><a href="/wiki/cesarz#Polish" title="cesarz">cesarz</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">emperor</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_7">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=67" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Scottish_Gaelic">Scottish Gaelic</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=83" title="Edit section: Scottish Gaelic">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_8">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=84" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Irish">Old Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sga"><a href="/wiki/cor#Old_Irish" title="cor">cor</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">act of putting</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, verbal noun of <i class="Latn mention" lang="sga"><a href="/wiki/foceird#Old_Irish" title="foceird">fo·ceird</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to put</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=87" title="Edit section: Adverb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="gd">car</strong>
</p>
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/somewhat" title="somewhat">somewhat</a>, <a href="/wiki/quite" title="quite">quite</a>, <a href="/wiki/rather" title="rather">rather</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="gd">Tha thu <b>car</b> fadalach.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You're somewhat late.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="gd">Thig an stòiridh gu ceann <b>car</b> obann.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The story came to an end somewhat abruptly.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=89" title="Edit section: Serbo-Croatian">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_9">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=90" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic language">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Slavic/c%C4%9Bsa%C5%99%D1%8C" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Slavic/cěsařь">*cěsařь</a></i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Slavic/c%D1%8Csar%D1%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Slavic/cьsarь (page does not exist)">*cьsarь</a></i>, from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Germanic languages">Germanic</a></span> language, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kaisaraz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kaisaraz">*kaisaraz</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/Caesar#Latin" title="Caesar">Caesar</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_9">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=91" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Serbo-Croatian_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Serbo-Croatian pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/t͡sâr/</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_12">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=92" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="sh">cȁr</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>Cyrillic spelling</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="sh"><a href="/wiki/%D1%86%D0%B0%D1%80#Serbo-Croatian" title="цар">ца̏р</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/czar" title="czar">czar</a>, <a href="/wiki/emperor" title="emperor">emperor</a>, <a href="/wiki/monarch" title="monarch">monarch</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="sh">Podajte <b>caru</b> carevo, a Bogu Božje.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Give the Emperor what belongs to the Emperor and God what belongs to God.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Slovene">Slovene</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=95" title="Edit section: Slovene">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_10">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=96" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh"><a href="/wiki/car#Serbo-Croatian" title="car">cȁr</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic language">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Slavic/c%C4%9Bsa%C5%99%D1%8C" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Slavic/cěsařь">*cěsařь</a></i>, from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Germanic languages">Germanic</a></span> language, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kaisaraz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kaisaraz">*kaisaraz</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/Caesar#Latin" title="Caesar">Caesar</a></i>.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_11">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=103" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_12">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=car&amp;action=edit&amp;section=111" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
